.

Agency.

  
**Default:** 0

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_TYPEHEURE.html#property_ID_TYPEHEURE)
ID\_TYPEHEURE

Int(11)

Unique identifier.

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_TYPEHEURE.html#property_TYPEH_ETAT)
TYPEH\_ETAT

Tinyint(1)

State :

*   `0` : Archived\_, if [TAB\_TYPEHEURE.TYPEH\_TYPEACTIVITE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_TYPEHEURE.html#property_TYPEH_TYPEACTIVITE)
     = 1 then "With alert if no absences request"\_
*   `1` : Current, if [TAB\_TYPEHEURE.TYPEH\_TYPEACTIVITE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_TYPEHEURE.html#property_TYPEH_TYPEACTIVITE)
     = 1 then "With alert if no absences request"\_
*   `2` : Archived & "Without alert if no absences request"_, only if [TAB\_TYPEHEURE.TYPEH\_TYPEACTIVITE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_TYPEHEURE.html#property_TYPEH_TYPEACTIVITE)
     = 1_
*   `3` : Current & "Without alert if no absences request"_, only if [TAB\_TYPEHEURE.TYPEH\_TYPEACTIVITE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_TYPEHEURE.html#property_TYPEH_TYPEACTIVITE)
     = 1_

  
**Default:** 1

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_TYPEHEURE.html#property_TYPEH_NAME)
TYPEH\_NAME

Varchar(250)

Name.

  
**Default:** ''

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_TYPEHEURE.html#property_TYPEH_ORDRE)
TYPEH\_ORDRE

Smallint

WorkUnitType order.

  
**Default:** 0

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_TYPEHEURE.html#property_TYPEH_PERMISSIONS)
TYPEH\_PERMISSIONS

Tinyint(1)

Access level :

*   `0` : Aucune ressource
*   `1` : Toutes les types de ressources
*   `2` : Certain types de ressources

  
**Default:** 0

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_TYPEHEURE.html#property_TYPEH_REF)
TYPEH\_REF

Int(11)

Reference.

  
**Default:** 0

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_TYPEHEURE.html#property_TYPEH_TYPEACTIVITE)
TYPEH\_TYPEACTIVITE

Tinyint(1)

Activity type :

*   `0` : Production
*   `1` : Absence
*   `2` : Internal
*   `3` : Exceptional - Time
*   `4` : Exceptional - Calendar

  
**Default:** 0

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_TYPEHEURE.html#property_TYPEH_TYPESRESSOURCES)
TYPEH\_TYPESRESSOURCES

[Text](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Text)

List of resource's types allowed.

It is a list of resource's types separated by `|` character.

A type's value is :

*   **integer** : [TAB\_PROFIL.PROFIL\_TYPE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_PROFIL.html#property_PROFIL_TYPE)
    

#### Example:

`"0|2|3|4"`

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_WEBSOCIAL.html#property_ID_PARENT)
ID\_PARENT

Int(11)

Entity's identifier :

*   Candidate : if [TAB\_WEBSOCIAL.WEBSOCIAL\_TYPE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_WEBSOCIAL.html#property_WEBSOCIAL_TYPE)
     is `0`_, cf. [TAB\_PROFIL.ID\_PROFIL](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_PROFIL.html#property_ID_PROFIL)
    _
*   Resource : if [TAB\_WEBSOCIAL.WEBSOCIAL\_TYPE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_WEBSOCIAL.html#property_WEBSOCIAL_TYPE)
     is `1`_, cf. [TAB\_PROFIL.ID\_PROFIL](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_PROFIL.html#property_ID_PROFIL)
    _
*   Contact : if [TAB\_WEBSOCIAL.WEBSOCIAL\_TYPE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_WEBSOCIAL.html#property_WEBSOCIAL_TYPE)
     is `2`_, cf. [TAB\_CRMCONTACT.ID\_CRMCONTACT](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_CRMCONTACT.html#property_ID_CRMCONTACT)
    _
*   Company : if [TAB\_WEBSOCIAL.WEBSOCIAL\_TYPE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_WEBSOCIAL.html#property_WEBSOCIAL_TYPE)
     is `3`_, cf. [TAB\_CRMSOCIETE.ID\_CRMSOCIETE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_CRMSOCIETE.html#property_ID_CRMSOCIETE)
    _

  
**Default:** 0

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_WEBSOCIAL.html#property_ID_WEBSOCIAL)
ID\_WEBSOCIAL

Int(11)

Unique identifier.

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_WEBSOCIAL.html#property_WEBSOCIAL_NETWORK)
WEBSOCIAL\_NETWORK

Tinyint(2)

Type :

*   `0` : Viadeo
*   `1` : Linkedin
*   `2` : Facebook
*   `3` : X

  
**Default:** 0

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_WEBSOCIAL.html#property_WEBSOCIAL_TYPE)
WEBSOCIAL\_TYPE

Tinyint(1)

Entity's type :

*   `0` : Candidate
*   `1` : Resource
*   `2` : Contact
*   `3` : Company

  
**Default:** 0

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_WEBSOCIAL.html#property_WEBSOCIAL_URL)

**Default:** ''

     = [TAB\_LISTETEMPS.ID\_LISTETEMPS](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_LISTETEMPS.html#property_ID_LISTETEMPS)
    
*   `1` : Expenses, [TAB\_VALIDATION.ID\_PARENT](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_VALIDATION.html#property_ID_PARENT)
     = [TAB\_LISTEFRAIS.ID\_LISTEFRAIS](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_LISTEFRAIS.html#property_ID_LISTEFRAIS)
    
*   `2` : Absences request, [TAB\_VALIDATION.ID\_PARENT](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_VALIDATION.html#property_ID_PARENT)
     = [TAB\_LISTEABSENCES.ID\_LISTEABSENCES](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_LISTEABSENCES.html#property_ID_LISTEABSENCES)
    

  
**Default:** 0

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USER.html#property_USER_ALLOW_PRODUCTION)

*   `1` : Customised
*   `0` : Disable

.

**Default:** ''

**Default:** 'Europe/Paris'

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USER.html#property_USER_TPSFRSETAT)
USER\_TPSFRSETAT

Tinyint(1)

Enable/disable the automatic creation and the email's sending of timesheets & expenses :

*   `3` : Enable only for timesheets
*   `2` : Enable only for expenses
*   `1` : Enable for both
*   `0` : Disable for both

  
**Default:** 1

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USER.html#property_USER_TPSFRSSTART)
USER\_TPSFRSSTART

[Date](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Date)

Starting date of timesheets & expenses entering.

This property can be `null`.

if `USER_TPSFRSSTART` is :

*   `null` : Hiring date, cf. [TAB\_CONTRAT](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_CONTRAT.html)
    
*   `3000-01-01` : Inactive
*   `YYYY-MM-01` : From the year & month indicated, 1970 <= `YYYY` <= 2038 and 1 <= `MM` <= 12

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USER.html#property_USER_TYPE)
USER\_TYPE

Tinyint(1)

Type :

*   `0` : Visitor
*   `2` : Manager
*   `4` : Administrator
*   `6` : Resource

  
**Default:** 0

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USER.html#property_USER_VALIDATIONABSENCES)
USER\_VALIDATIONABSENCES

Varchar(250)

Requests of absences validation circuit.

This property can be `null`_, accordingly the default's validation circuit will be the one of user's agency [TAB\_GROUPECONFIG.GRPCONF\_VALIDATIONABSENCES](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_GROUPECONFIG.html#property_GRPCONF_VALIDATIONABSENCES)
_.

If `USER_VALIDATIONABSENCES<>null` then it is a list of validator separated by `|` character.

A validator's value is :

*   **integer** : [TAB\_USER.ID\_USER](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USER.html#property_ID_USER)
    _, obligatorily the unique identifier of another user_
*   `0` : Manager N
*   `-1` : Manager N+1
*   `-2` : Manager N+2
*   `-3` : Manager N+3

  
**Default:** null

#### Example:

`"0|-1|100"`

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USER.html#property_USER_VALIDATIONFRAIS)
USER\_VALIDATIONFRAIS

Varchar(250)

Expenses validation circuit.

This property can be `null`_, accordingly the default's validation circuit will be the one of user's agency [TAB\_GROUPECONFIG.GRPCONF\_VALIDATIONFRAIS](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_GROUPECONFIG.html#property_GRPCONF_VALIDATIONFRAIS)
_.

If `USER_VALIDATIONFRAIS<>null` then it is a list of validator separated by `|` character.

A validator's value is :

*   **integer** : [TAB\_USER.ID\_USER](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USER.html#property_ID_USER)
    _, obligatorily the unique identifier of another user_
*   `0` : Manager N
*   `-1` : Manager N+1
*   `-2` : Manager N+2
*   `-3` : Manager N+3

  
**Default:** null

#### Example:

`"0|-1|100"`

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USER.html#property_USER_VALIDATIONTEMPS)
USER\_VALIDATIONTEMPS

Varchar(250)

Timesheets validation circuit.

This property can be `null`_, accordingly the default's validation circuit will be the one of user's agency [TAB\_GROUPECONFIG.property\_GRPCONF\_VALIDATIONTEMPS](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_GROUPECONFIG.html#property_property_GRPCONF_VALIDATIONTEMPS)
_.

If `USER_VALIDATIONTEMPS<>null` then it is a list of validator separated by `|` character.

A `validator` value can be :

*   **integer** : [TAB\_USER.ID\_USER](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USER.html#property_ID_USER)
    _, obligatorily the unique identifier of another user_
*   `0` : Manager N
*   `-1` : Manager N+1
*   `-2` : Manager N+2
*   `-3` : Manager N+3

  
**Default:** null

#### Example:

`"0|-1|100"`

ID\_PARENT

Int(11)

Entity's identifier :

*   If [TAB\_REGLEEXCEPTION.PARENT\_TYPE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_REGLEEXCEPTION.html#property_PARENT_TYPE)
     = `0` then [TAB\_SOCIETE.ID\_SOCIETE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_SOCIETE.html#property_ID_SOCIETE)
    
*   If [TAB\_REGLEEXCEPTION.PARENT\_TYPE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_REGLEEXCEPTION.html#property_PARENT_TYPE)
     = `1` then [TAB\_CRMSOCIETE.ID\_CRMSOCIETE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_CRMSOCIETE.html#property_CSOC_BAREMESEXCEPTION)

Int(11)

Unique identifier.

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_REGLEEXCEPTION.html#property_PARENT_TYPE)
PARENT\_TYPE

Tinyint(1)

Entity's type :

*   `0` : Agency
*   `1` : Company

  
**Default:** 0

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_REGLEEXCEPTION.html#property_REGLE_BAREMEREF)
REGLE\_BAREMEREF

Int(11)

Scale's reference :

*   If [TAB\_REGLEEXCEPTION.PARENT\_TYPE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_REGLEEXCEPTION.html#property_PARENT_TYPE)
     = `0` then see [TAB\_GROUPECONFIG.GRPCONF\_BAREMESEXCEPTION](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_GROUPECONFIG.html#property_GRPCONF_BAREMESEXCEPTION)
    
*   If [TAB\_REGLEEXCEPTION.PARENT\_TYPE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_REGLEEXCEPTION.html#property_PARENT_TYPE)
     = `1` then see [TAB\_CRMSOCIETE.CSOC\_BAREMESEXCEPTION](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_CRMSOCIETE.html#property_CSOC_BAREMESEXCEPTION)
    

  
**Default:** 0

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_REGLEEXCEPTION.html#property_REGLE_COUT)
REGLE\_COUT

Decimal(30,10)

Cost :

*   If the scale is composed with calendar activities then it is _gross salary in the agency's currency_
*   If the scale is composed with time activities then it is _rate of hourly salary_

  
**Default:** 0

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_REGLEEXCEPTION.html#property_REGLE_ETAT)
REGLE\_ETAT

Tinyint(1)

State :

*   `0` : Archived
*   `1` : Current

  
**Default:** 1

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_REGLEEXCEPTION.html#property_REGLE_NAME)
REGLE\_NAME

Varchar(250)

Name.

  
**Default:** ''

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_REGLEEXCEPTION.html#property_REGLE_REF)
REGLE\_REF

Int(11)

Reference.

  
**Default:** 0

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_REGLEEXCEPTION.html#property_REGLE_TARIF)
REGLE\_TARIF

Decimal(30,10)

Price :

*   If the scale is composed with calendar activities then it is _price excludind tax in the agency's currency_
*   If the scale is composed with time activities then it is _rate of hourly price excluding tax_

  
**Default:** 0

*   `1` : Enable
*   `0` : Disable

  
**Default:** 0

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USERCONFIG.html#property_CONFIG_MENUBAR)
CONFIG\_MENUBAR

[Text](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Text)

List of ordered modules & apps available in the Front-End :

*   `dashboard` : Dashboard view
*   `resources` : Resources view
*   `candidates` : Candidates view
*   `products` : Products view
*   `opportunities` : Opportunities view
*   `actions` : Actions view
*   `positionings` : Positionings view
*   `contacts` : Contacts view
*   `companies` : Companies view
*   `projects` : Projets view
*   `timesReports` : Timesheets view
*   `expensesReports` : Expenses view
*   `absencesReports` : Requests of absences view
*   `purchases` : Purchases view
*   `payments` : Payments view
*   `deliveries` : Deliveries view
*   `orders` : Orders view
*   `invoices` : Invoices view
*   `billingDeliveriesPurchasesBalance` : Billing deliveries & purchases balance view
*   `billingMonthlyBalance` : Billing monthly balance view
*   `billingProjectsBalance` : Billing projects balance view
*   `billingSchedulesBalance` : Billing schedules balance view
*   `activityReports/productionPlans` : Production plans of activity reports view
*   `activityReports/reporting` : Reporting of activity reports view
*   `activityReports/distributionCompanies` : Distribution companies of activity reports view
*   `activityReports/projects` : Projects of activity reports view
*   `activityReports/resources` : Resources of activity reports view
*   `integer` : [TAB\_INSTALLAPI.ID\_MAINAPI](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_INSTALLAPI.html#property_ID_MAINAPI)
     of App

Modules & apps are separated by `|` character.

#### Example:

`"dashboard|actions|resources|candidates|contacts|companies"`

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USERCONFIG.html#property_CONFIG_NOTIFCENTER_ACTIVITY_ABS_DELETED)
CONFIG\_NOTIFCENTER\_ACTIVITY\_ABS\_DELETED

Smallint(6) unsigned

Define the notification channels for deleted absence 0 - disabled Bitwise operation over the following values : 1 = Notification ; 2 = Email; 4 = Mobile Ex : 7 = 1 + 2 + 4 = Notification + email + Mobile

  
**Default:** 7

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USERCONFIG.html#property_CONFIG_POLES)

     of pole are separated by `|` character

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USERCONFIG.html#property_CONFIG_POSITIONING_SUGGEST)
CONFIG\_POSITIONING\_SUGGEST

[Text](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Text)

Positioning suggest settings (json) : All settings for positioning suggest. All allowed attributes are mapped in PositioningSuggest model

  
**Default:** '{}'

#### Example:

`{"defaultPositioningSuggestCandidatesPerimeter" : 1, "defaultPositioningSuggestResourcesPerimeter" : 1, "defaultPositioningSuggestExcludedCandidatesTypes" : [1], "defaultPositioningSuggestExcludedResourcesTypes" : [1], "defaultPositioningSuggestExcludedCandidatesStates" : [3], "defaultPositioningSuggestExcludedResourcesStates" : [0], "defaultPositioningSuggestKeywordsFromOpportunity" : ["title", "tools"], "defaultPositioningSuggestFiltersFromOpportunity" : ["tools", "domains"]}`

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USERCONFIG.html#property_CONFIG_REPARTITION)
CONFIG\_REPARTITION

[Text](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Text)

List of indicators for the distribution companies of activity reports

*   These indicators can be `-1` that **designed a separator**
*   These indicators can be, those which value is \[0,1,2,3,6,7,8,9,13,14,15,17,18,19,23,24,27,28\], in commercial reporting of activity reports, prefixed by `AC_`
*   These indicators can be, those which value is \[3,4,5\] in human resources reporting of activity reports, prefixed by `RH_`
*   These indicators can be, those which value is \[0,1,2,3\] in activity & expenses reporting of activity reports, prefixed by `TF_`
*   These indicators can be, those which value is \[1\] in billing reporting of activity reports, prefixed by `FN_`

Indicators are separated by `|` character.

#### Example:

`"AC_0|RH_3|TF_0|FN_1"`

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USERCONFIG.html#property_CONFIG_REPORTINGAC)
CONFIG\_REPORTINGAC

[Text](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Text)

List of indicators for the commercial reporting of activity reports :

*   `-1` : **Designed a separator**
*   `0` : Signed turnover
*   `1` : Total weighted turnover of opportunities
*   `2` : Signed costs
*   `3` : Signed margin
*   `4` : Signed profitability
*   `5` : Total number of projects created
*   `6` : Total number of projects in progress
*   `7` : Total number of deliveries in progress
*   `8` : Total number of opportunities
*   `9` : Total number of positionings
*   `10_integer` : Total number of contacts actions for each `integer` type where `integer` worths all [TAB\_ACTION.ACTION\_TYPE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_ACTION.html#property_ACTION_TYPE)
     values except notification
*   `11` : Total number of deliveries started up
*   `12` : Total number of deliveries stopped
*   `13` : Estimated turnover
*   `14` : Estimated costs
*   `15` : Estimated margin
*   `16` : Estimated profitability
*   `17` : Total turnover
*   `18` : Total costs
*   `19` : Total margin
*   `20` : Total profitability
*   `21_integer` : Total number of opportunities actions for each `integer` type where `integer` worths all [TAB\_ACTION.ACTION\_TYPE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_ACTION.html#property_ACTION_TYPE)
     values except notification
*   `22_integer` : Total number of projects actions for each `integer` type where `integer` worths all [TAB\_ACTION.ACTION\_TYPE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_ACTION.html#property_ACTION_TYPE)
     values except notification
*   `23` : Number of technical assistance projects in progress
*   `24` : Number of packages projects in progress
*   `25` : Rate of technical assistance projects in progress
*   `26` : Rate of packages projects in progress
*   `27` : Number of recruitment done
*   `28` : Number of products projects in progress
*   `29` : Rate of products projects in progress
*   `30` : Rate of recruitment
*   `31_integer` : Weighted turnover opportunities for each `integer` state where `integer` worths all key **id** for JSON response **data.setting.state.opportunity** of [API /application/dictionary](https://support.boondmanager.com/hc/fr/articles/209465606-Introduction)
    
*   `32` : Total number of contacts created
*   `33` : Total number of companies created
*   `34_integer` : Total number of opportunities created for each `integer` state where `integer` worths all key **id** for JSON response **data.setting.state.opportunity** of [API /application/dictionary](https://support.boondmanager.com/hc/fr/articles/209465606-Introduction)
    

Indicators are separated by `|` character.

#### Example:

`"0|2|3|-1|4|-1|34_0|34_1|34_1|-1|8"`

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USERCONFIG.html#property_CONFIG_REPORTINGAG)
CONFIG\_REPORTINGAG

[Text](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Text)

List of indicators for the global reporting of activity reports :

*   `-1` : **Designed a separator**
*   `0` : Signed turnover
*   `1` : Real costs
*   `2` : Margin
*   `3` : Profitability
*   `4` : Paid turnover
*   `5` : Paid contributive margin
*   `6` : Paid contributive profitability
*   `7` : Administrative costs
*   `8` : Paid exploitation margin
*   `9` : Paid exploitation profitability
*   `10` : Invoiced turnover
*   `11` : Invoiced contributive margin
*   `12` : Invoiced contributive profitability
*   `13` : Invoiced exploitation margin
*   `14` : Invoiced exploitation profitability
*   `15` : Production turnover
*   `16` : Production contributive margin
*   `17` : Production contributive profitability
*   `18` : Production exploitation margin
*   `19` : Production exploitation profitability
*   `20` : Purchases costs
*   `21` : Total purchases costs

Indicators are separated by `|` character.

  
**Default:** ''

#### Example:

`"0|1|2|3"`

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USERCONFIG.html#property_CONFIG_REPORTINGAR)
CONFIG\_REPORTINGAR

[Text](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Text)

List of indicators for the recruitment reporting of activity reports :

*   `-1` : **Designed a separator**
*   `0` : Total number of candidates created
*   `1_integer` : Total number of candidates actions for each `integer` type where `integer` worths all [TAB\_ACTION.ACTION\_TYPE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_ACTION.html#property_ACTION_TYPE)
     values except notification
*   `2` : Total number of candidates positioned
*   `3_integer` : Total number of candidates created for each `integer` state where `integer` worths all key **id** for JSON response **data.setting.state.candidate** of [API /application/dictionary](https://support.boondmanager.com/hc/fr/articles/209465606-Introduction)
    
*   `4_integer` : Total number of candidates created for each `integer` source where `integer` worths all key **id** for JSON response **data.setting.source** of [API /application/dictionary](https://support.boondmanager.com/hc/fr/articles/209465606-Introduction)
    

Indicators are separated by `|` character.

  
**Default:** ''

#### Example:

`"1_0|1_1|1_2|-1|0|-1|3_0|3_1|3_2"`

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USERCONFIG.html#property_CONFIG_REPORTINGCMP)
CONFIG\_REPORTINGCMP

[Text](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Text)

Indicators for the resources of activity reports :

*   `-1` : **Designed a separator**
*   `0` : Number of working days
*   `1` : Ordered production activity per project
*   `2` : Planned production activity per project
*   `3` : Taken production activity per project
*   `4` : Total ordered production activity
*   `5` : Total planned production activity
*   `6` : Total taken production activity
*   `7` : Total ordered absence activity
*   `8` : Total planned absence activity
*   `9` : Total taken absence activity
*   `10` : Total ordered internal activity
*   `11` : Total planned internal activity
*   `12` : Total taken internal activity
*   `13` : Occupation rate ordered
*   `14` : Occupation rate planned
*   `15` : Occupation rate taken
*   `16` : Loading rate ordered
*   `17` : Loading rate planned
*   `18` : Loading rate taken
*   `19` : Availability ordered
*   `20` : Availability planned
*   `21` : Availability taken
*   `22` : Rest budget ordered to plan
*   `23` : Rest budget ordered to take
*   `24` : Signed turnover
*   `25` : Signed costs
*   `26` : Signed margin
*   `27` : Signed profitability
*   `28` : Production turnover
*   `29` : Real costs
*   `30` : Production real margin
*   `31` : Production real profitability
*   `32` : Signed, planned production activity per project
*   `33` : Signed, taken production activity per project
*   `34` : Planned turnover
*   `35` : Planned costs
*   `36` : Planned margin
*   `37` : Planned profitability
*   `38` : Costs signed internal activity
*   `39` : Costs planned internal activity
*   `40` : Costs taken internal activity
*   `41` : Costs signed absence activity
*   `42` : Costs planned absence activity
*   `43` : Costs taken absence activity
*   `44` : Number of working days from J+1
*   `45` : Number of working days until J
*   `46` : Planned production activity from J+1 per project
*   `47` : Taken production activity until J per project
*   `48` : Total planned production activity from J+1
*   `49` : Total taken production activity until J
*   `50` : Total planned absence activity from J+1
*   `51` : Total taken absence activity until J
*   `52` : Total planned internal activity from J+1
*   `53` : Total taken internal activity until J
*   `54` : Occupation rate planned from J+1
*   `55` : Occupation rate taken until J
*   `56` : Loading rate planned from J+1
*   `57` : Loading rate taken until J
*   `58` : Availability planned from J+1
*   `59` : Availability taken until J
*   `60` : Signed production per project
*   `61` : Total signed production activity
*   `62` : Total signed absence activity
*   `63` : Total signed internal activity
*   `64` : Occupation rate signed
*   `65` : Loading rate signed
*   `66` : Availability signed
*   `67` : Rest budget signed to plan
*   `68` : Rest budget signed to take
*   `69` : Hourly exceptional time per project
*   `70` : Calendar exceptional time per project
*   `71` : Total hourly exceptional time
*   `72` : Total calendar exceptional time

Indicators are separated by `|` character.

#### Example:

`"0|1|2|3"`

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USERCONFIG.html#property_CONFIG_REPORTINGFN)
CONFIG\_REPORTINGFN

[Text](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Text)

List of indicators for the billing reporting of activity reports :

*   `-1` : **Designed a separator**
*   `0` : Turnover
*   `1` : Total turnover invoiced
*   `2` : Total turnover ordered
*   `3` : Total delta invoiced
*   `4` : Total turnover of invoiced orders
*   `5` : Proforma turnover

Indicators are separated by `|` character.

  
**Default:** ''

#### Example:

`"0|1|2|3"`

*   `-1` : **Designed a separator**

*   `2` : Type

*   `4` : Advancement ordered taken
*   `5` : Rest budget ordered to take

*   `8` : Paid turnover

*   `10` : Paid real margin
*   `11` : Paid real profitability

*   `13` : End

*   `15` : Ordered turnover
*   `16` : Delta invoiced
*   `17` : Production turnover

*   `20` : Global costs

*   `24` : Invoiced real profitability

*   `49` : Advancement signed taken
*   `50` : Rest budget signed to take

*   `52` : Hourly exceptional time per resource
*   `53` : Calendar exceptional time per resource
*   `54` : Total hourly exceptional time
*   `55` : Total calendar exceptional time
*   `56` : Area of expertise

Indicators are separated by `|` character.

#### Example:

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USERCONFIG.html#property_CONFIG_REPORTINGRH)
CONFIG\_REPORTINGRH

[Text](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Text)

List of indicators for the human resources reporting of activity reports :

*   `-1` : **Designed a separator**
*   `0` : Total number of internal resources
*   `1` : Number of hiring
*   `2` : Number of departures
*   `3` : Total number of resources on delivery
*   `4` : Number of external resources on delivery
*   `5` : Number of internal resources on delivery
*   `6` : Number of resources on internal activity
*   `7` : Number of resources on absence activity
*   `8_integer` : Total number of resources actions for each `integer` type where `integer` worths all [TAB\_ACTION.ACTION\_TYPE](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_ACTION.html#property_ACTION_TYPE)
     values except notification
*   `9` : Cost of internal activity
*   `10` : Cost of absence activity
*   `11` : Duration of internal activity
*   `12` : Duration of absence activity
*   `13` : Occupation rate
*   `14` : Internal activity rate
*   `15` : Total number of resources positioned
*   `16` : Total costs of resources
*   `17` : Total number of external resources

Indicators are separated by `|` character.

  
**Default:** ''

#### Example:

`"4|5|6|7|-1|0|17|-1|8_4|8_5|8_8"`

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USERCONFIG.html#property_CONFIG_REPORTINGTF)
CONFIG\_REPORTINGTF

[Text](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Text)

List of indicators for the activity & expenses reporting of activity reports :

*   `-1` : **Designed a separator**
*   `0` : Total duration of signed time
*   `1` : Total duration of taken time
*   `2` : Total costs of signed expenses
*   `3` : Total costs of taken expenses
*   `4` : Number of timesheets validated
*   `5` : Number of timesheets rejected
*   `6` : Number of timesheets unvalidated
*   `7` : Number of expenses validated
*   `8` : Number of expenses rejected
*   `9` : Number of expenses unvalidated
*   `10` : Number of requests of absences validated
*   `11` : Number of requests of absences rejected
*   `12` : Number of requests of absences unvalidated
*   `13` : Total duration of planned time
*   `14` : Total duration of normal & exceptional taken time
*   `15` : Duration of taken time
*   `16` : Total costs of normal & exceptional taken time
*   `17` : Costs of taken time

Indicators are separated by `|` character.

  
**Default:** ''

#### Example:

`"0|1|-1|2|3"`

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_USERCONFIG.html#property_CONFIG_TYPELIEUXDEFAULTWEEK)
CONFIG\_TYPELIEUXDEFAULTWEEK

[Text](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Text)

Workplaces times settings (json) : Array of settings. Each item of array contains the settings for one workplaceType (reference and agency). For each workplaceType, an array named "days" contains each duration for each day (duration and dayOfWeek in literal english notation)

#### Example:

`[{"workplaceType":{"reference":1,"agency":{"id":"1"}},"days":[{"duration":1,"dayOfWeek":"monday"},{"duration":1,"dayOfWeek":"tuesday"}]},{"workplaceType":{"reference":2,"agency":{"id":"1"}},"days":[{"duration":1,"dayOfWeek":"wednesday"},{"duration":1,"dayOfWeek":"thursday"},{"duration":1,"dayOfWeek":"friday"}]}]`

.

Account\*, only if settings doesn't belong to a role\*.

  
**Default:** 0

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_PROFIL.html#property_PARAM_TYPEDISPO)
PARAM\_TYPEDISPO

Int(11)

Availability's type.

*   If **Resource** :
    
    *   `1`: Available immediately _(Availability **is synced** with project updates)_
    *   `2`: Available after [PARAM\_DATEDISPO](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_PROFIL.html#property_DATE_DISPO)
         _(Availability **is synced** with project updates)_
    *   `3`: Available immediately _(Availability **is not sync** with project updates)_
    *   `4`: Available after [PARAM\_DATEDISPO](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_PROFIL.html#property_DATE_DISPO)
         _(Availability **is not synced** with project updates)_
*   If **Candidate** :
    
    *   `9`: Available after [PARAM\_DATEDISPO](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_PROFIL.html#property_DATE_DISPO)
        
    *   `-1`: Not defined
    *   or _cf. key **id** for JSON response **data.setting.availability** of [API /application/dictionary](https://support.boondmanager.com/hc/fr/articles/209465606-Introduction)
        _

  
**Default:** 0

### [](https://doc.boondmanager.com/bddboondmanager/classes/TAB_PROFIL.html#property_PARAM_TYPESOURCE)
PARAM\_TYPESOURCE

Int(11)

_

**Only for candidates**

  
**Default:** -1
